# <a name="com-error-codes-comadmin-filter-graphics"></a><span data-ttu-id="f7d61-104">Codici di errore COM (COMAdmin, FILTER, GRAPHICS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-104">COM Error Codes (COMADMIN, FILTER, GRAPHICS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f7d61-105">Nella tabella seguente viene fornito un elenco di codici di errore utilizzati dalle API basate su COM.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-105">The following table provides a list of error codes used by COM-based APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f7d61-106">Se si verificano problemi con un'applicazione che si sta installando o eseguendo, contattare il supporto tecnico per il software che Visualizza il messaggio di errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-106">If you are experiencing difficulty with an application you are installing or running, contact customer support for the software that is displaying the error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-107">Per ottenere supporto per un prodotto Microsoft, vedere [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-107">To obtain support for a Microsoft product, go to [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go).</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-108">Costante/valore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-108">Constant/value</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-109">Descrizione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-109">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|:--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|:--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span id="COMADMIN_E_OBJECTERRORS"></span><span id="comadmin_e_objecterrors"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-110"><dt>**COMadmin \_ E \_ OBJECTERRORS**</dt> <dt>0x80110401</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-110"><dt>**COMADMIN\_E\_OBJECTERRORS**</dt> <dt>0x80110401</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                                                                                  | <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-111">Errori durante l'accesso a uno o più oggetti. la raccolta ErrorInfo potrebbe avere più dettagli</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-111">Errors occurred accessing one or more objects - the ErrorInfo collection may have more detail</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |

| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_INTERNAL_ERROR"></span><span id="error_graphics_internal_error"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-850"><dt>**Errore \_ \_ \_ Errore interno di grafica**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E7</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-850"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_INTERNAL\_ERROR**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E7</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                                                               | <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-851">Un errore interno ha causato l'esito negativo di un'operazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-851">An internal error caused an operation to fail.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_SESSION_TYPE_CHANGE_IN_PROGRESS"></span><span id="error_graphics_session_type_change_in_progress"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-852"><dt>**Errore \_ \_ \_ \_ Modifica del tipo di sessione grafica \_ in \_ corso**</dt> <dt>0xC02605E8</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-852"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_SESSION\_TYPE\_CHANGE\_IN\_PROGRESS**</dt> <dt>0xC02605E8</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                         | <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-853">La funzione non è riuscita perché la sessione corrente sta cambiando il tipo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-853">The function failed because the current session is changing its type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-854">Questa funzione non può essere chiamata quando la sessione corrente sta cambiando il relativo tipo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-854">This function cannot be called when the current session is changing its type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f7d61-855">Attualmente sono disponibili tre tipi di sessioni: console, Disconnected e remote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7d61-855">There are currently three types of sessions: console, disconnected and remote.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
